DOM event dispatch system in Firefox (mozilla/gecko-dev) follows the W3C DOM specification for event dispatching. Here is the complete chain:\\n\\n### 1. Event Creation (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:1419-1483)\\n`EventDispatcher::CreateEvent()` is the factory function that creates DOM Event objects from WidgetEvent structures. It maps widget event classes (eMouseEventClass, eKeyboardEventClass, etc.) to their corresponding DOM event types (MouseEvent, KeyboardEvent, etc.) and instantiates the appropriate event object using NS_NewDOM* constructor functions.\\n\\n### 2. Event Target Identification & Chain Construction (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:869-1178)\\n`EventDispatcher::Dispatch()` is the main entry point that:\\n- Sets the event target (aEvent->mTarget)\\n- Creates the event target chain by iteratively calling `GetEventTargetParent()` on each target and its parent (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:1009-1139)\\n- Handles event retargeting for shadow DOM and native anonymous content\\n- Marks the event as being dispatched (aEvent->mFlags.mIsBeingDispatched = true)\\n\\nThe event target chain is built as an array of `EventTargetChainItem` objects (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:125-424), with each item representing a target in the event path from the original target up through the document tree.\\n\\n### 3. Capture/Bubble Phase Traversal (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:491-689)\\n`EventTargetChainItem::HandleEventTargetChain()` orchestrates the event flow through three phases:\\n\\n**Capture Phase (lines 516-585)**: Iterates from the root target down to the original target in reverse order, calling `HandleEvent()` on each item if propagation is not stopped. Sets mInCapturePhase=true.\\n\\n**Target Phase (lines 587-611)**: Calls `HandleEvent()` on the original target itself, first in bubble phase context, then with mInTargetPhase=true.\\n\\n**Bubble Phase (lines 613-648)**: Iterates from the original target back up through parent targets (if event.bubbles=true), calling `HandleEvent()` on each item. Sets mInBubblingPhase=true.\\n\\nAfter the default event group, the system event group is dispatched (lines 651-688) through the same three phases, which allows system event listeners and the actual default action handling to occur.\\n\\n### 4. Event Listener Invocation (dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp:1233-1295)\\nWhen `EventTargetChainItem::HandleEvent()` is called (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:339-370), it:\\n1. Calls `mTarget->WillHandleEvent()` if requested\\n2. Retrieves the `EventListenerManager` for the current target\\n3. Calls `EventListenerManager::HandleEvent()` which delegates to `HandleEventInternal()` (line 364-366)\\n\\n`EventListenerManager::HandleEventInternal()` (dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp:1439-1534) looks up all registered listeners for the event type by:\\n1. Finding \\\"all events\\\" listeners\\n2. Finding type-specific listeners (e.g., listeners for \\\"click\\\")\\n3. Calling `HandleEventWithListenerArray()` for each listener array (lines 1481-1514)\\n\\n`EventListenerManager::HandleEventWithListenerArray()` (dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp:1536+) iterates through the listener array and calls `HandleEventSingleListener()` for each listener.\\n\\n`EventListenerManager::HandleEventSingleListener()` (dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp:1233-1295) performs the actual listener invocation:\\n1. Sets event.currentTarget\\n2. Sets the event's passive listener state (line 1243)\\n3. For JS event handlers: compiles the event handler if it's a string (lines 1259-1262)\\n4. Invokes the listener's HandleEvent method (lines 1274-1283):\\n   - For WebIDL callbacks: calls `listenerHolder.GetWebIDLCallback()->HandleEvent()`\\n   - For XPCOM callbacks: calls `listenerHolder.GetXPCOMCallback()->HandleEvent()`\\n5. Clears currentTarget\\n6. Sets mExceptionWasRaised flag if the handler threw (line 1291)\\n\\n### 5. Default Action Execution (dom/events/EventStateManager.cpp:3977+)\\nAfter all event listeners have been invoked, `EventTargetChainItem::PostHandleEvent()` (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:483-489) delegates to `EventTarget->PostHandleEvent()`.\\n\\nFor most HTML elements, this calls into `EventStateManager::PostHandleEvent()` (dom/events/EventStateManager.cpp:3977+), which implements the default browser behaviors:\\n\\n- **For eMouseDown** (lines 4008-4151):\\n  - Handles focus management (finding the focusable element to focus)\\n  - Manages capturing content for drag operations\\n  - Updates click count tracking\\n\\n- **For eMouseUp** (lines 4152+):\\n  - Fires click events if the element is still under the mouse\\n  - Handles activation behaviors\\n  - Updates element states\\n\\n- **For eClick**:\\n  - Triggers navigation for links\\n  - Submits forms\\n  - Toggles checkboxes/radio buttons\\n\\nOther events like eKeyDown, eFocus, eBlur also have default behaviors implemented in PostHandleEvent().\\n\\n### Event Flow Summary for a Click Event:\\n\\n1. Platform sends WidgetMouseEvent to PresShell\\n2. PresShell::HandleEventWithTarget() calls EventDispatcher::Dispatch()\\n3. EventDispatcher builds event target chain from clicked element to document root\\n4. EventDispatcher::CreateEvent() creates a MouseEvent DOM object\\n5. For each phase (capture → target → bubble):\\n   - Iterate through event target chain\\n   - Call HandleEvent() which invokes EventListenerManager\\n   - EventListenerManager calls each registered listener's callback\\n   - Event can be canceled via preventDefault()\\n6. System event group listeners are invoked\\n7. EventStateManager::PostHandleEvent() executes default actions:\\n   - Focus management\\n   - Link navigation\\n   - Form submission\\n   - Element activation\\n\\nThis architecture ensures compliance with the W3C DOM Event specification while allowing Firefox to manage browser-specific behaviors and maintain separation between content scripts (default event group) and system operations (system event group).\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":5,"cache_creation_input_tokens":283,"cache_read_input_tokens":64999,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":283},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"067ed368-5f34-47c1-904b-3626072b0374","uuid":"6e559886-4458-41b5-9952-265dadfe597b"}
